## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of current population P and time t. Population dynamics models range from simple exponential/logistic growth to more complex forms involving Allee effects, time-dependent carrying capacities, and multi-regime dynamics.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate declines logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (minimum viable population threshold)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * (c1 * P)**c3 (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t * P (logistic with time-dependent environment)
- Exponential with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 (growth with constant removal)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (generalized density-dependent growth)
- Von Bertalanffy type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Periodic carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))) (seasonal environment)
- Weak Allee logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P**2 * (1 - c1 * P) (cooperative growth at low density)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (general cubic population model)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative quadratic term in P (e.g., -c*P^2) → density-dependent competition / carrying capacity limitation
- Growth rate proportional to P at low density → per-capita growth rate is approximately constant (exponential regime)
- Growth rate proportional to P^2 at low density → Allee effect / cooperative behavior requiring minimum population
- Logarithmic dependence on P (e.g., log(c/P)) → Gompertz-type growth with multiplicative decline in per-capita rate
- Rational form P/(1+cP) → contest competition where resources are shared but saturate
- Cubic terms in P (P*(P-a)*(K-P)) → bistability with both extinction and carrying capacity as stable states
- Time-dependent coefficients (e.g., c*sin(t)) → seasonally forced or periodically varying environment
- dP_dt/P analysis (per-capita rate) being linear in P → classical logistic; nonlinear → generalized models
- Sign change in dP_dt at specific P values → equilibrium points / carrying capacity / Allee thresholds
- Additive constant term independent of P → immigration/emigration or constant harvesting/stocking
